GLOBAL_MAP GEN/COLORS-> tiles are populated by 4x4 colors, mixed areas = Ecotone/transition area
Part_1: 
	DEPTHS: Dark Blue: Represents the deepest water (abyssal plains and ocean trenches).
	-> Gen one Ocean -> break into 10 plates (5 subduction/Basalt plates, 5 rising/Granite plates) -> set Force Score to every plate and Movement_Direction + Movement_Direction -> (No adjacent plate can have same direction.)
				#-> Plates lose 1 Force_Score every time they move ->	Growth dissapates outward though Volcanic Activity 
			Subduction_Zone =  Initial  -> at Subduction_Zone where Granite and Basalt meet add +1 Land_Tile all adjacent tiles, +.5 height to current tile (subduction zone) & all adjacent tiles-> 
					-> For every Subduction_Zone collision expand Land_Mass +1 in all directions from the indside, pushing tiles outward. add +1 Rift Score to pushed tiles	 
			Conduction_zone =  	2 GRANITE_PLATES fuse at a +1 height rate as +1 Land_Mass creation occurs, 
				if Tile/peak is +9 distribute + 1 height to all adjacent tiles, expand Land_Mass +1 in all directions
					if 2 adjacent plates/Land_Mass have 1 opposing Move_Direction add + 1 Friction_Score to every touching tile per turn = Fault_Line -> if same Type
						Every tile with +2 Friction adds +1 Friction to all adjacent tiles
							if Fricion = 100, Earthquake
				Earthquake -> if RiftScore = 100, Land Mass  = New Continental_Plate ->  Break from Subduction_Zone/Land_Mass next active-turn (Based on Plate Velocity)
							Set move Direction away from Subduction_Zone/Land_Mass and Force_Score = 100, Speed = remaining Land_Mass speed
					Plates lose -1 Force_Score per Movement, -1 Speed_Score per collision
						Collision Interaction -> Opposing Directions Cancel and generate -2 extra speed reduction
									 Same Directions are Additive and generate + 1/-1 to the Directional Vector, adding a spin/drift
					If no Gen Timer Set End when all Force_Scores = 0

SHALLOWS: Light Blue: Represents shallow water, continental shelves, or areas near the coastline.
	
	
	BIOME GEN - CLIMATE MAP
			HEAT_CLIMATE_MAP_Cause: [BaseTile_HeatScore = ([GlobalTerrainTile_Height (x) -1]+ 10)]
						+ [BaseEquator_HeatScore = -> 10 (#max heat) (x) 12.10], where x = static, y = Drift Rate= sin(decant degree)/current time				
				+					Seasonal_Heat_Focus = Midpoint_Y + (sin(Current_Time * DR) * Max_Drift_Distance) Max_Drift_Distance = 15
			WIND_CLIMATE_MAP: = Tiles over 10 HEAT dipserse 1 heat to coldest neighbor until Tile_HeatScore = BaseTile_HeatScore, everytime a tile disperses heat increase its Wind_Score +1
						Wind_Score increases Heat disperse +1 per score and dispersal range +1 [so Wind_Score +2 adds +3heat to coldest tile (C) adjacent to the coldest tile (B) touching the current tile (A) ] 
							if gains HEAT + 1 decrease tile WIND_SCORE + 1 -> If  tile WIND_SCORE = -1 add +2 Heat to tile
				=
			MOISTURE_CLIMATE_MAP: Water tiles add 1 Water_Content to adjacent tiles during HEAT_MOVEMENT (Wind_Climate_Map).
				+		If Moisture_Content -> [Water_Content + Tile_HeatScore] ≥ 20 -> Water_Content = Rainfall_TypeA
			HEAT_CLIMATE_MAP	Rainfall_TypeA dipserse 2 heat & 1 Water_Content to coldest neighbor until Tile_HeatScore = BaseTile_HeatScore 
						Adjacent Tiles to Rainfall_TypeA tiles recieve Rainfall_TypeB = dipserse 1 heat & .5 Water_Content to coldest neighbor until Tile_HeatScore = BaseTile_HeatScore ->
				=			if Rainfall_TypeA is not triggered -> Rainfall on tile triggers Liquid_Height +1 & accumulates every turn until Rainfall ceases -> 
								if tile A has Liquid_Height +1 -> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is Lower Water moves from tile A to B
												-> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is same look for Lower tile	
													-> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is same & no Lower tile -> if tile A Liquid_Height +2 move +1 Liquid from tile A to B if B = empty
														if tile A has Liquid_Height +2 or more -> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is same & no Lower tile or empty tile B
														-> if tile B = Liquid_Height +1 & tile C = Liquid_Height +2 -> Move +1 Liquid from tile A to C 
															-> if Liquid_Height exceeds +3 disperse +1 to all adjcent tiles, & reduce GlobalTerrainTile_Height -1-> restart collection ->once all rivers have outlets = Waterway_Map 	
			AVGRAINFALL_CLIMATE_MAP: After waterway gen, rain map is passed over water map = FLOODPLAIN_CLIMATE_MAP -> Where any tile that collects +3 water = Bedrock, & 
				+														FERTILE Active Flood + Moderate/High Heat.
			WATERWAY_WORLD_MAP													CLAY	High Rainfall + No Flood + Low Drainage.			
																		LOAMY	Moderate Rainfall + Moderate Heat	
																		SANDY	Low Rainfall + High Heat

 
WATER-BODIES: Blue/Cyan: Indicates mid-depth water and larger inland bodies.
	[LAKES,WATERWAYS ]	


LOWLANDS: Denotes lowlands and plains (altitudes near 0–200 meters). Even a desert like the Mojave may be dark green if it is at a low elevation.
	[PLAINS, VALLEY, DUNE, BASIN, COASTAL PLAIN, WETLANDS (SWAMP, MARSH, FOG,BEN), SHORE, RIVERBANK]
RISING TERRIAN: Light Green: Represents low hills or rising terrain (roughly 200–500 meters).
HIGHLANDS/PLATUEAS: Yellow/Tan: Indicates plateaus or mid-height hills (500–1,000 meters).
	[HILLS,PLATEU, MESA, BUTTE]
MOUNTIAN/PEAK: Brown/Red-Brown: Represents mountainous regions (1,000–3,000 meters); darker browns indicate higher ranges.
	[MOUNTAIN_RANGE, CLIFF, CANYON, PEAK,]
SNOW-FIELD/GLACIER: White: Denotes the highest peaks and permanent glaciers or snowfields (typically over 3,000 meters). 
	[SNOW CAPPED PEAKS, ICEFIELD, GLACIER]



CANOPY_HEIGHT_MAP:

# CLIMATE HEIGHT RANGES (The Base Variable)
# Determined by [Water_Content + Heat_Score] interaction within the ClimateEnum.

[TROPICAL / SUBTROPICAL] 
- Requirement: [Water_Content + Heat_Score] ≥ 25
- Range: 22.0m - 35.0m (Subtropical leans toward lower bound; Tropical toward upper)
- 4x4 Render: High Density (12-16/16). Multi-layer sprite stacks (Understory + Emergent).

[TEMPERATE_HUMID / MEDITERRANEAN]
- Requirement: High Water_Content + Moderate/High Heat
- Range: 20.0m - 30.5m (Humid can spike to 40m+ in Coastal variants)
- 4x4 Render: High Density (10-14/16). Large crown Hardwood/Conifer sprites.

[TEMPERATE]
- Requirement: Moderate Water_Content + Moderate Heat
- Range: 15.0m - 25.0m
- 4x4 Render: Moderate Density (8-12/16). Balanced mix of deciduous/evergreen.

[ARID]
- Requirement: [WIND_SCORE = -1] + [Heat_Score > 10] (High Heat / Low Water)
- Range: 5.0m - 12.0m 
- 4x4 Render: Sparse/Bimodal (2-6/16). Clumped Succulent and Dry-Shrub sprites.

[ARCTIC]
- Requirement: [BaseTile_HeatScore] < 2 (Maximum Heat Sink)
- Range: 0.27m - 5.0m
- 4x4 Render: Ground-cover (Moss/Algae). Sparse, low-profile Taiga/Tundra sprites.

[AQUATIC]
- Requirement: [Liquid_Height] > 0
- Range: 0.0m - 5.0m (Submerged/Surface)
- 4x4 Render: Water-Fern/Algae sprites. Height is restricted by Depth/Shallows score.


# 2. HEMISPHERIC DRIFT MODIFIERS (The Scaling Rule)
# Uses [BaseEquator_HeatScore] and [Latitude] to apply quadratic variance.

[SOUTHERN_HEMISPHERE] (Latitude < 0)
- Rule: Strong Latitudinal Dependence (R² = 67.1%)
- Calculation: Final_Height = Base_Height * (1.0 - (Latitude^2))
- Result: Predictable, sharp decline in canopy height as you move toward the South Pole.

[NORTHERN_HEMISPHERE] (Latitude > 0)
- Rule: Localized Climate Relationship (R² = 35.3%)
- Calculation: Final_Height = Base_Height * (0.67 + (Local_Moisture_Modifier * 0.33))
- Result: Greater variance; local "Heat Pockets" (like Mediterranean zones) can maintain height despite higher latitude.

UNIFED-EVENT/(GRAMMAR)/(SENTNCE)-GENERATION RULES
																							
------Model---------(5w+h1)
Who (Agent/ACTOR[(N/N-I)]): O-d/(Agent/ENACTED[N/N-I])
What (Agent/ENACTED[N/N-I]): O-i/ (Agent-Action/ACTOR/ENACTED[(InteractVerb)]
When: Specific: Time +/or Date, NonSpecific: at, in, on, before, after, during, since, until, by
"Where: Specific: Location (in, on, at, under, above, below, beside, between, 
                    near, by, inside, outside, over), NonSpecific: Direction: to, after, ahead of, before"
Why(reason/cause)(descriptive only): Because (before noun/N-I), for, due to, because of (before pronoun/N-I), from-> (Emotional State verb or Mental IntentVerb)
How (Method/modifier (of-v)): with, by 
--------Nouns----------
Noun Types- Proper: [N-P]Person, [N-L]Place, [N-O]Thing, if Idea N-I=[N-P, N-L, N-O]																									

remedy typically refers to solving a practical problem, harm, or illness
amends refers to making reparation, compensation, or apology 
-----------------------------------------------------------------
UNIFIED EVENT GRAMMAR: COMPLETE FOUNDATION

Core sentence structure:
simple (command): Verb(V) + Noun(N)
simple (descriptive): Noun(N) + Verb(V)
Standard (command: V + O-i +O-d
Standard (descriptive: N + V + Object(O-d)[secondary noun direct-object]
Complex (command/direct):  V-i + O-i + V-d + O-d
Complex (descriptive): N + V + Object(O-i)[tertiary noun indirect-object] + O-d
Complex (command/inderect/multi-act): V-n + V-i + O-i + V-d + O-d
Complex (descriptive/inderect/multi-act): N + V-i + O-i + V-d + O-d
Simple Question (Inverse): V-aux + N + V
Standard Question (Inverse): V-aux + N + V + O-d
Complex Question (Inverse): V-aux + N + V-i + O-i + V-d + O-d
noun = subject, verb=action, Object(S)= noun/subject (direct or indirect) direct = acted upon/action committed to, indirect = acted through

General rule type 2:REACTION CHAIN
Actor 1(5w+h1)[Initiator/original actor ] = Who1-  Initial roll Role Context [Positive, Negative, Neutral]->[Who1-0[N-P/N-I/Actor]]->[What1-0[Verb]]->[When1-0[Specific/NonSpec]]->[Where1-0[Specific/NonSpec]]->[Why1-0+conjunction[Emotional State verb or Mental IntentVerb]]->How1[optional/rolled[Who1-2[with N-P/N-I[Actor3], by[N-P/N-I/Actor3('s involvement)]/What1-1[with N-O/N-I]/by[Depends on What1/connontation rules]]]

Enatced 2(3w)[Reciever/Differectly affected/interacted with[What1 occurs to]] = Who2 -> Rolled[Who2-0[N-P/N-I/Enacted]]/[What2-0[N-O/N-I/Enacted]]->What2-2[Result/Reaction[roll for veb type- if Mechanical [= Actor - Enacted->Action Outcome[What1-3]],Alt[]
																					      if Movement[= Actor - Enacted->Actors next Action [What1-2]],[]
																					      if Manual/Interaction/Communication/Mental Intent/Ownership/Daily-Living [= Actor - Enacted->Affected Outcome Remedy[What[3-3](Future)=Goal->Relational/Action]],Alt[[What[3-0](Reaction)=Goal->Relational/Action]]]
																					      if Cognition/EmotionalState [= Actor - Enacted->Action Outcome Mystery[What[3-3](Future)=Goal->Info-Related]],Alt[Action Outcome Mystery[What[3-0](Reaction)=Goal->Info-Related]]
																					      if Perception/Aux [= Actor - Enacted->Affected Outcome Mystery [What[3-3](Future)=Goal->Info-Related -> verb roll = Cognition/EmotionalState]], Alt[Affected Outcome Mystery[What[3-0](Reaction)= Goal->Info-Related -> verb roll = Cognition/EmotionalState]
																					      if Relational/State/Linking [= Actor - Enacted->Roll Affected[3(5w+h1)]->links to[What3-3]], Alt[Roll Affected[3(5w+h1)]->links to[What3-0]]

Affected[Can be Enacted[Who2/N-I]] 3(5w+h1) = Who3->Current[Who3-0[N-P/N-I/Actor]]->Reaction[What3-0[InteractionVerb]]->Reaction[When3-0[Specific/NonSpec]]->Reaction[Where3-0[Specific/NonSpec]]-> How3[rolled[Who3-2[with N-P/N-I[Actor4], by[N-P/N-I/Actor4('s involvement)]/What3-2[with N-O/N-I]/by[What 3-3]]

Where:Who - 1 = Primary Actor
	    2 = Enacted-> Indirect Actor/Links Actor & Affected
	    3 = Affected - Primary Reciever
	    Reaction = Future/Planned Action

Where/in conjunction with:
      - 0 = primary (Primary Intent/Core)
      - 1 = directlylinked-to-primary(Direct Link/Instrument)
      - 2 = tertiary-to-primary(Tertiary/Environmental)
      - 3 = result/state change -> 3-3 Ends chain/Generates for both parties, known values replace rolls

GRAMMAR Ruleset(s):

Noun : Names a person, place, thing, or idea/Pronoun: Replaces a Topic noun after topic established
Name N-N: Specific Person, Place, Object/Idea
Object (T): non specific thing to varying degrees: sword or cutlass vs Name: Eternal Cutlass of Riverforge
Pronoun: non-direct person or thing (ex. him, it, that): By type/Case/Role key- A/BNOUN= After/before noun, A/BVERB= Afterr/before verb, ALE = Standalone
Subjective-Singular = PRNSS: [I - ACTOR] [You - ENACTED] [He - TOPIC/MALE] [She - TOPIC/MALE] [It - TOPIC/THING/IDEA]
Subjective-Plural = PRNSP: [We - ACTOR + ENACTED] [You - ENACTED + TOPIC] [THEY - THING/IDEA + TOPIC]
Objective-Singular = PRNOS: [Me - ACTOR] [You - ENACTED] [Him - TOPIC/MALE] [Her - TOPIC/MALE] [It - TOPIC/THING/IDEA]
Objective-Plural = PRNOP: [Us - ACTOR + ENACTED] [You - ENACTED + TOPIC] [THEM - THING/IDEA + TOPIC]
Possessive-Singular = PRNPS: [My - ACTOR/BNOUN] [Mine - ACTOR/AVERB/ALE] [Your - ENACTED] [His - TOPIC/MALE] [Hers - TOPIC/MALE] [Its - TOPIC/THING/IDEA]
Possessive-Plural = PRNPP: [Our - ACTOR + ENACTED/BNOUN] [Ours - ACTOR + ENACTED/AVERB/ALE] [You - ENACTED + TOPIC] [THEM - THING/IDEA + TOPIC]
Reflexive-Singular = PRNRS: [Myself - ACTOR]  [Yourself - ENACTED] [Himself- TOPIC/MALE] [Herself- TOPIC/MALE] [Itself - TOPIC/THING/IDEA]
Reflexive-Plural = PRNRP: [ [Ourselves- ACTOR]  [Yourselves - ENACTED] [Themselves- TOPIC/THING/IDEA/]

Adjective: : Describes or modifies a noun or pronoun 
Descriptive: good, bad, happy, sad, big, small, blue, red, beautiful, difficult, easy, new, old, pretty, tall, short, kind, nice, wonderful
Quantitative: many, few, several, one, two, three, four, first, second, third, all, some, most
Demonstrative: this, that, these, those
Proper Adjectives: American, European, Italian, French, Spanish

Adverb: Modifies a verb, adjective, or another adverb
Manner (How): quickly, slowly, carefully, well, badly, loudly, gently, easily, rapidly, hungrily
Time (When): now, soon, yesterday, tomorrow, always, often, never, before, after, late, early, still
Place (Where): here, there, everywhere, inside, outside, up, down, near, far, home, somewhere, nowhere
Degree (How much/extent): very, extremely, almost, quite, too, enough, really, nearly, less, more

Preposition: Shows the relationship between a noun/pronoun and other words (e.g., in, on, under).Links Verb and Object
ex. Simple (command: V + P + [N = (O-d)]
"Where: Specific: Location (in, on, at, under, above, below, beside, between, behind, across, 
                    near, by, inside, outside, over), NonSpecific: Direction: to, after, ahead of, before"
When: Specific: Time +/or Date, NonSpecific: at, in, on, before, after, during, since, until, by
How (Method/modifier (of-v)): with, by, without 
Why (reason/cause)(descriptive only): Because (before noun), for, due to, because of (before pronoun), from
Who (Agent/ACTOR[(N)]): O-d
What (Agent/ENACTED[N]): O-i
Ownership: relates O-d to O-i, of, of the, ('s)
Measure: quantity 

Verb: Shows an action, occurrence, or state of being (Verb tags define context toinfer Connotation)
Pronoun Type-Perspective/case (verb Tag)
Verb Target [specifc type of noun affect. Person Place or thing](Verb tag)
Verb connotaion (Verb tag)/Verb Speech Type(Verb Tag): NEGATIVE, POSITIVE, NEUTRAL
Verb Reaction (expected/main)
	(-)+(+) = (-)
	(+) + (-) = (+)
	(+) + (+) = (+)
	(-) + (-) = (+)
	Neutral = functions as 0
->Formula - (1)-(ACTOR/Observer (or quest giver) goal[tied to verb])
		+ 
	    (2)-(ENACTED (goal)) = OUTCOME 
		->(For quest,  Quest Giver = ACTOR)
			(for indv-ACTOR(characters) (+) ENACTED = OUTCOME(ENACTED reaction)]"
	OUTCOME - ACTOR + ENACTOR = OUTCOME (inverse AO = - EO when opposed, = when aligned)

Conjunction: Connects words, phrases, or clauses [Modifier or Qualifier*not gameply logic]
CONJUNCTION RULE (FINALIZED)
"Conjunctions may appear:
- between verbs
- between clauses
- between objects
- between full sentence structures"
Conjunctions **modify or qualify** the relationship between actions.
FUNCTIONS:
	1. **Action chaining**
		V-d + Conj + V-d
		“attack AND steal”
	2. **Temporal sequencing**
		Clause + Conj + Clause
		“help merchant BEFORE bandits arrive”
	3. **Causality**
		Clause + Conj + Clause
		“villager fled BECAUSE wolves attacked”
	4. **Conditional logic**
		Conj + Clause
		“IF bandits attack, guard intervenes”
	5. **Multi‑act expansion**
		(N + V + O-d) + Conj + (N + V + O-d)
	6. **Qualifier insertion**
		Conj modifies meaning:
		“help merchant BUT refuse payment”
Conjunction-type
Conjunction: Coordinatings, Subordinating, Correlative][Verbs: Auxiliary/Helping Verbs
Coordinatings: for, and, nor, but, or, yet, so
Subordinating: because, although, if, while, after, before, since, when, unless, until, how, tha
Correlative: either/or, neither/nor, both/and, not only/but also, whether/or

Morphology-.Morhpemes (each speech part needs morrpheme catgeory by type)
Morphology-1. Nouns: Number and Ownership
		Pluralization: Most nouns add -s or -es (e.g., dog → dogs, wish → wishes). Scribendi
		#Possession: Singular nouns add -’s (kitten’s), while plural nouns typically add only an apostrophe if they already end in ""s"" (kittens’). QuillBot
Morphology-2. Verbs: Tense and Agreement
		Third-Person Singular: Adding -s or -es to indicate present tense (e.g., I go → He goes). 
		Past Tense: Adding -ed or -d for regular verbs (e.g., walk → walked). YouTube: 
3. Adjectives: Intensity (Comparison)
Adjectives use suffixes to show degrees of comparison. Grammarly
Comparative: Adding -er to compare two things (e.g., fast → faster). EF United States
Superlative: Adding -est to indicate the highest degree in a group (e.g., fast → fastest). Albert.io
Spelling Shifts: If an adjective ends in -y, it changes to -i before the suffix (happy → happier). Lingo Apps


5.Adverbs are almost always formed by adding a suffix to a base word (usually an adjective). Wordy
Derivational Suffixes:
-ly: The most common way to turn an adjective into an adverb (e.g., quick → quickly, quiet → quietly). GINGER
-wise: Added to nouns to show direction or manner (e.g., clockwise, lengthwise, otherwise). Scribd
-ward(s): Added to indicate direction (e.g., backward, homeward, upwards). Scribd
Spelling Rules for "-ly":
If the base ends in -y, it changes to -i (e.g., happy → happily). My English Class
If it ends in -le, drop the -e and add -y (e.g., gentle → gently). My English Class
If it ends in -ic, add -ally (e.g., tragic → tragically). My English Class

Participial Prepositions: Verbs modified with an -ing or -ed suffix that have evolved to function as prepositions. 
Considering (e.g., ""Considering the weather..."")
Concerning (e.g., ""Questions concerning the law..."")
Provided (e.g., ""Provided that you stay..."")


Generative-Ruleset:

Noun Types-  Person, Place Thing
Verb Types - Movement, Manual, Daily Living, Interaction, Communication, Mechanical, Vigorous, Cognition, Emotional State, Mental Intent, Perception, Ownership, Relational/State

"Where: Specific: Location (in, on, at, under, above, below, beside, between, behind, across, 
                    near, by, inside, outside, over), NonSpecific: Direction: to, after, ahead of, before"
When: Specific: Time +/or Date, NonSpecific: at, in, on, before, after, during, since, until, by
How (Method/modifier (of-v)): with, by 
Why (reason/cause)(descriptive only): Because (before noun), for, due to, because of (before pronoun), from
Who (Agent/ACTOR[(N)]): O-d
What (Agent/ENACTED[N]): O-i



for max-multistage- setences- Topic  = event ( who + what + when + where + why) = MMS
MMS =  Each part of event gets a sentence (capped 3 layer)[Ex. Topic1 -> Who1  (Topic2 = Topic1 cause)->Who(Topic2 reason)

Markov Chain Specification

DOM- Documnt Model Object
RootNode: 
Element: 
LeafNodes: Word chain + punct.

MSInt- Markov Integration

KgramMap: {W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1}}
rules: 
	if W_n = Sentence Ender (.)(!)(?)(;)(")(...) add all to previous map
			IF W_n in [., !, ?, ;, ", ...] 
  				THEN Append(W_n) TO Map({W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1}})

	if W_n = Pause (,)(-)(`)(~) add W_4

	if W_n = Apostrophe ->  W_n(-1) + (') + W_n(+1)
			W_{n-1} + ' + W_{n+1} -> Single Token

	if W_n = Numeric -> Add W_n+1 to W_n
			Numeric: W_n + W_{n+1} -> Single Token

	 if W_n = Uppercase_and does not follow Sentence Ender W_n = Name/Title/P-N
Extraction:
	if W_n = Sub_Break (()({)([)(*)
		if Sub_Break = (()({)([)
			Inv_Sub_Break = ())(})(])
		Sub_Break + W_n(x) + Inv_Sub_Break -> Single Extraction Token
	THEN APPEND EXTRACTION (W_n) TO Map({W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1}})

Discard: 
	if W_n = (//)(\\)(--)(**)(&&)(##)(@@)
		Then skip
	if W_n = (@)
		W_n = "At" -> if Map({W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1}}= singular instance, skip append
	if W_n = (&) 
		W_n = "And" -> if Map({W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1}}= singular instance, skip append
	if W_n = (%)
		W_n = "Percent" -> if W_{n-1}= "Numeric" 
					W_n + "Percent"  -> Single Token
				-> else W_n = "Percentage" 
	if W_n =($)
		W_n = "Currency"	
				
KgramMap_return:
K_Frequency: Returns the occurrence count of this specific token.

KgramMap_AuthorityA: Single/Numeric[-string] word weighting

Occurence: +1
Uppercase: +A
Lowercase: +B
Exclamation: +E

       Weight: P'_w = (Count(w) + Auth(w)) / (Sum_{v in S} (Count(v) + Auth(v)))

KgramMap_AuthorityB: String weighting

Occurence: +1
Numeric conflict = Avg of conflict
	If Count(W_n_Numeric) > 1 for Kgram(K):
    		Target_Weight = Average(AuthA(W_n_1) + AuthA(W_n_2)...)
    			Apply Target_Weight to all W_n in Conflict

KgramMap_AuthorityC: String-Additions
State1_Occurence: Initial ({W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1}
State2_Occurence: Appened ({W_{n-3}, W_{n-2}, W_{n-1} + W_n(x)

  		CONDENSTION, #["Creates Peptide/Glycosidic bonds; releases H2O. (Collagen, Cellulose, Silk)]
      		ADDITION, #[Chain growth via radical/enzymatic activation; no byproduct. (Certain Resins/Lipids)]
#[Termination_n]
      FIXED, #[n is a constant blueprint (e.g., Collagen n≈1050). Result: Uniformity.]
      ENVIRONMENTAL, #[n stops based on resource/climate availability. Result: Divergent Growth.",REGIONAL- avg Caloric Value of vegetation - avg CALORIC Need of Species- [Avg Need of Competitors], Competitors = Same diet + Predators
      LINKS, #[Chains bond laterally (e.g., Keratin with Sulfur). Result: High Hardness/Toughness]
#[Genotypes]
    #Fidelity
      FIDELITY_MULIPLIER, #[1.2x Texture_Intensity]
      FIDELITY_EXPRESSION, #[QUALITY:links to adjectives]
    #Velocity
      VELOCITY_MULIPLIER, "0.75x Growth_Time",
      VELOCITY_EXPRESSION, "Rapid assembly of 'n' at the cost of durability; prone to 'Defects' trait."
}

enum Genetic_Formation_Logic {
#[Development: Core_Blueprint]
  INHERITANCE, #["2 sets of chromosomes -1 from each parent" are provided; only one set determines initial trait expression. (Autosomes 1-22, Sex Chromosome 23)]
  EXPRESSION, #["Phenotype = Build, Appearance, Race, Genetic-Conditions, Genetic-Mutations"] are determined by the selected genes and their interactions.
  POLYPLOIDY, #["Number of chromosome sets"] which determines baseline size and fertility characteristics of the species. (e.g., Diploid 2n, Tetraploid 4n).

#[Material_Synthesis: Stages]
  CONDENSATION_SYNTHESIS, #["Creates Peptide/Glycosidic bonds; releases H2O."] Mechanism for creating structural proteins like **Collagen Type I**, **Alpha-Keratin**, and **Cellulose**.
  ADDITION_SYNTHESIS, #["Chain growth via radical/enzymatic activation; no byproduct."] Mechanism for creating lipids, **Squalene**, and many specific alkaloids like **Caffeine** and **Morphine**.
  LINKING_SYNTHESIS, #["Chains bond laterally (e.g., Keratin with Sulfur)."] Mechanism used for strong structural components like **Beta-Keratin**, **Peptidoglycan**, and **Calcium Carbonate** composites.

#[Genetic_Result: Trait_Stability]
  FIXED_TRAIT, #["n is a constant blueprint"] where the material length/expression is a constant genetic property (e.g., Collagen, Chitin). Result: Uniformity.
  ENVIRONMENTAL_TRAIT, #["n stops based on resource/climate availability"] where expression is modulated by external factors (e.g., Lanolin, Hemicellulose, Body Fat). Result: Divergent Growth.

#[Mutation_Logic]
    #Outcomes
      BENEFICIAL, #[25% Base Chance: Expands magnitude range upward, grants increased resistance.]
      NEUTRAL,    #[50% Base Chance: Color variation, no mechanical effect.]
      HARMFUL,    #[25% Base Chance: Reduces magnitude range, grants disease susceptibility, developmental defects.]
    #Triggers
      CHANCE_ROLL, #["If slot filled with 2 'non-can-fill'-> Chance Mutation is rolled".]
      DE_NOVO,     #["Spontaneous (De Novo): (0.6% to 0.7%)" chance for new mutations not inherited from parents.]
}

enum Metabolic_Logic {#Genetic-Homeostasis-trait
#[Pathway: Energy_Transformation]
    ANABOLIC,   #["Construction phase; consumes ATP to synthesize complex biomass (Growth/Repair/Storage)."]
    CATABOLIC,  #["Destruction phase; breaks down substrates (Glucose/Lipids) to yield ATP/Heat."]

#[Regulation: Enzyme_Kinetics]
    CONSTITUTIVE, #["Always ON; Baseline metabolites required for cellular life (e.g., Glycolysis)."]
    FACULTATIVE,  #["Trigger-based; activated by In Utero signals or external stress (e.g., Ketosis)."]

#[Termination_Flux]
    HOMEOSTATIC,  #["Fixed set-point; metabolite levels return to a genetic baseline (n=Normal range)."]
    ALLOSTATIC,   #["Variable set-point; adjusts 'n' based on systemic load/threat (e.g., Adrenaline spikes)."]

#[Genetic_Properties]
    #Efficiency (The "Metabolic Engine" Quality)
    EFFICIENCY_MULTIPLIER, #[1.5x ATP_Yield per unit Substrate. Result: High Endurance.]
    THERMAL_EXPRESSION,    #[HEAT_WASTE:links to adjectives (Endothermic vs Ectothermic)]

    #Specialization (The "Chemical Arsenal")
    XENO_DISSIPATION,      #[VELOCITY: Rate of toxin neutralisation. Result: Poison Resistance.]
    SECONDARY_SYNTHESIS,   #[BIO-UNIQUE: Species-specific compounds (e.g., Venoms, Pheromones, Vitamin-C synthesis).]

#[Environmental_Bias]
    RESOURCE_SCARCITY,    #[THRESHOLD: Reduces Basal Metabolic Rate (BMR) to conserve 'n' units.]
    ABUNDANCE_PLASTICITY, #[THRESHOLD: Increases Lipid_Sequestration (Storage) relative to Caloric_Surplus.]
}
enum MetaboliteReceptors {
    // Amines/Alkaloids
    NICOTINE_RECEPTOR, #[Agonist: Nicotine][Effect: Neurotoxic/Stimulant][Method: MaterialComponents.ELECTRICITY.Voltage]

    // General Metabolites/Toxins (from PDF data)

    LACTIC_ACID_RECEPTOR, #[Agonist: Lactic_Acid][LinkedBodyPart: Muscle][Effect: Metabolic][Method: MaterialComponents.FORM.Rigidity]

    GLUTAMATE_RECEPTOR, #[Agonist: Glutamate][Effect: Excitatory/Plasticity (+)]
    GABA_RECEPTOR, #[Agonist: GABA][Effect: Inhibitory/Sedation (-)]

}

enum Shapes  {#MAGIC specific
#SHAPES: [Vertex 0 = (0,0 point of origin) ,Vertex x = (convergence/termination points)]
	NONE,
	PROJECTILE,
	RAY,
	BEAM,
	PARALLEL_BEAM,
	DIVERGENT_BEAM,
	CONVERGENT_BEAM,
	ORB,
	CUBE,
	LUNE,
	TETRAHEDRON,
	TESSERACT,
	HYPERSPHERE,
};

enum Shapes_Subclass {#CRAFTING AND MAGIC

#PROJECTILE
	ARROWHEAD, #[Arrowhead: Length > Width; Depth < 10% Width (Flattened triangular mass)]
	TEARDROP, #[Teardrop: Base Width = Base Height; Length > Width (Radial base to point taper)]
	BLADE, #[Blade: Length >> Width; height < 5% Width]
	CONE, #[Cone: Height > Width (Tapered 3D volume)]
	SLUG, #[Slug: Height = Width (Balanced mass)]		

#CUBE
 	BOX, #[Box: Height = Width = Depth (CORED; Wall < 10% Width)] #If it has volume.
	BLOCK, #[Block: Height = Width = Depth] #If it is solid and heavy.
#SQUARE
	SLAB, #[Slab: Width & Length >> Depth]		
	FRAME, #[Frame: Width = Length; Center Void > 50% Area (CORED; Perimeter only)]			
	PARTITION, #[Screen: Width = Length; Mass/Void = Interdependent (FLUTED; Permeable plane)]
#SPHERE		
	BALL, #[Ball: Radius = 1 ]			
	SHELL, #[Shell: Radius = 1; Wall < 10% Radius (CORED; Enclosure)]			
	LATTICE, #[Lattice: Radius = 1; Mass < 50% Volume (FLUTED; Structural sphere)]
#CIRLCE
	DISK, #[Disk: Diameter = 1]		
	RING, #[Ring: Diameter = 1; Void > 70% Area (CORED; Pure boundary)]			
	WHEEL, #[Wheel: Diameter = 1; Void/Mass = Structural balance (FLUTED; Radial interface)]
#CYLINDER	
	FILAMENT, #[Filament: Length > 3x Radius (SOLID; Longitudinal mass)]
	TUBE, #[Tube: Length > 3x Radius; Wall < 20% Radius (CORED; Longitudinal passage)]	
#LUNE
 	CRESCENT, #[Half_Moon: Arc Thickness < 10% Radius (CORED; Thin arc-skin)] #Frequently used because the moon's phases are the most recognizable examples of this geometry.
	SICKLE, #[Sickle: Arc Thickness > 20% Radius (SOLID; Weighted curve)] #Used if the curve is sharp or suggests a hook-like quality.

#TETRAHEDRON
	TIP, #[Tip: Vertex = x (The point of convergence)]			
	MOLD, #[Mold: Length > Height (CORED; Negative triangular volume)]# to split or hold something.]			
	TRUSS, #[Truss: Length > Height (FLUTED; Triangular skeleton)]
#TRIANGLE/TIP
	WEDGE, #[Wedge: Length > Height (SOLID; The inclined plane)]
	POINT, #[Point: Length >> Width (The potential for penetration)]# used to Pierce
},

const FILAMENT_TEXTILE_CLASS = {
	"FINE_FIBER":  {"MIN": 0.01, "MAX": 0.05}, # <0.5mm
	"SMALL_FIBER": {"MIN": 0.05, "MAX": 0.10}, # 0.5mm - 1mm
	"FIBER":       {"MIN": 0.10, "MAX": 0.80}, # 1mm - 8mm
	"THICK_FIBER": {"MIN": 0.15, "MAX": 0.50}  # 1.5mm - 5mm
}
 
const FILAMENT_TEXTILE_CLASS = {
	"FINE_FIBER":  {"MIN": 0.01, "MAX": 0.05}, # <0.5mm
	"SMALL_FIBER": {"MIN": 0.05, "MAX": 0.10}, # 0.5mm - 1mm
	"FIBER":       {"MIN": 0.10, "MAX": 0.80}, # 1mm - 8mm
	"THICK_FIBER": {"MIN": 0.15, "MAX": 0.50}  # 1.5mm - 5mm
}  





Typical Fiber/Yarn Thickness: FILAMENT TEXTILE CLASSIFICATION = 
Sewing: Fine thread, <0.5mm (often as fine as 0.1–0.3mm) = FINE_FIBER
Stitching: Slightly thicker, but still fine, 0.5mm to 1mm = SMALL_FIBER
Braiding: 1mm+ (cords/ropes commonly 2–8mm)		= FIBER
Knitting: 1.5mm (fine)–5mm (bulky); most usage 2–4mm = THICK_FIBER


Fastener Shear & Stability (L/W/H Logic)
The stability of a Composite is determined by the Fastener Grade relative to the Part Dimensions.
Fastener	Physics Role	Strength Formula (Sim Logic)
Rivet	Shear Specialist	Strength = (Material_Hardness * Rivet_Area) * Vibration_Modifier(1.0)
Screw	Tension/Torque	Strength = (Thread_Depth * Clamp_Force) * Vibration_Modifier(0.8)
Rope/String	Tensile Binding	Strength = (Tensile_Limit * Knot_Efficiency) * Elasticity_Modifier(< 1.0) [Base_Knot_Efficiency = SURVIVAL SKILL x .5]
Nail Strength Formula: Strength = (Material_Hardness * Surface_Area) * Friction_Coefficient
Stability Logic: Joint_Stability = (Sum_Fastener_Strength) / (Part_Mass * Distance_from_Center).


|ITEM_STATS	| SHAPED, MOLDED, CORED, FLUTED, FLUTED_CORE, BOUND, EDGE, EDGE_TYPE, BLUNT, BLADED, DAMAGE, DAMAGE_TYPE, KINETIC, EDGE_SLASH, EDGE_PIERCE, VERTICIES, VERTEX_0, VERTEX_X, VERTEX_Y, BLADE_EDGE, SHARPNESS, BLADE_COMP, SIZE, SMALL, REGULAR, GREAT, WIDTH, NARROW, NORMAL, BROAD, TEXTILE_FILAMENT, FINE_FIBER, SMALL_FIBER, FIBER, THICK_FIBER": {"MIN": 0.15, "MAX": 0.50}  # 1.5mm - 5mm

Vertex 0 = (0,0 point of origin)
Vertex x = (convergence/termination points)
Vertex y = (convergence/termination points)

# PROJECTILE
Slug: Height = Width (Balanced mass)
Cone: Height > Width (Tapered 3D volume)
Arrowhead: Length > Width; Depth < 10% Width (Flattened triangular mass)
Blade: Length >> Width; Depth < 5% Width (Extreme longitudinal extension)
Teardrop: Base Width = Base Height; Length > Width (Radial base to point taper)

# CUBE / SQUARE
Block: Height = Width = Depth (Uniform 3D mass)
Box: Height = Width = Depth (CORED; Wall < 10% Width)
Slab: Width & Length >> Depth (Flat independent mass)
Frame: Width = Length; Center Void > 50% Area (CORED; Perimeter only)
Partition: Width = Length; Mass/Void = Interdependent (FLUTED; Permeable plane)

# SPHERE
Ball: Radius = 1 (SOLID; 100% Fill)
Shell: Radius = 1; Wall < 10% Radius (CORED; Enclosure)
Lattice: Radius = 1; Mass < 50% Volume (FLUTED; Structural sphere)

# CIRCLE
Disk: Diameter = 1 (SOLID; 100% Fill)
Ring: Diameter = 1; Void > 70% Area (CORED; Pure boundary)
Wheel: Diameter = 1; Void/Mass = Structural balance (FLUTED; Radial interface)

# CYLINDER
Rod: Length > 3x Radius (SOLID; Longitudinal mass)
Tube: Length > 3x Radius; Wall < 20% Radius (CORED; Longitudinal passage)

# LUNE
Sickle: Arc Thickness > 20% Radius (SOLID; Weighted curve)
Half_Moon: Arc Thickness < 10% Radius (CORED; Thin arc-skin)

# TETRAHEDRON / TRIANGLE
Tip: Vertex = x (The point of convergence)
Wedge: Length > Height (SOLID; The inclined plane)
Mold: Length > Height (CORED; Negative triangular volume)
Truss: Length > Height (FLUTED; Triangular skeleton)
Point: Length >> Width (The potential for penetration)

enum DIFFICULTY_TYPE {#NAMED BY AETHER SATURATION
	DIFFICULTY
	NONE, #[DISABLE AETHER_CHEMICALELEMENT]
	STORM, #[AETHER ONLY OCCURS IN AREA AFFECTED BY AETHER STORMS]
	FLOOD, #[REGULAR MODE]
},

enum UNIVERSAL {#CONNOTATION/ENERGY_TYPE
	POSITIVE,
	NEGATIVE,
	NEUTRAL,
	CONNOTATION,
	ENERGY_TYPE,
},

	"CONNOTATION": ["POSITIVE", "NEGATIVE", "NEUTRAL"]
	"ENERGY_TYPE": ["POSITIVE", "NEGATIVE"]
},
---------------------------------------------------ACTIONS & BUTTONS------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
enum MAINMENU_ACTIONBAR {#MENU NESTING FOR CONTEXT INTERACTIONS, IF  ACTION REQUIRES TIMER-> PLAYER SET= BONUS RULES, AUTO= NO  BONUS/ 1st time craft = x2 work time by type, meaning the first sword you make takes  twice as long as normal
	MOVEMENT,
	INTERACTION, #ENTERS LOOK FOR TARGETING.-> TARGET DISPLAY IN BOX ON RIGHT SIDE OF WINDOW, IF ENTITY OR ITEM ON GROUND TILE (GET LARGEST BY DEFAULT)
	INVENTORY,
#COMBAT_INITIATION
	UNSHEATHE, #ARMED
	SHEATHE, #HANDS DOWN/ PUT UP WEAPON
	FIGHT, #UNARMED 
	RELAX, #HANDS DOWN/DOES NOT PUT UP WEAPON
},

enum JOURNL_MENU {
#INFORMATION_TABS
	WORLD_INFO_TAB,	 #PEOPLE, ITEMS, PLACES, EVENTS
CHANGETO jutsu, KNOWLEDGE_TAB, 	#SKILLS , INTENTS, TECHNIQUES Quick-Slots -base = 9 + 1 reserve [Combat, Control = increase slot "base"(10 slots)]-> COMBOS (precomposed Attacks) -> Abilities (precomposed Spells/Activations)
#	INVENTORY,										   		   
	CONVO_TAB, #BARTER, DEEP MODE-> CONTEXT BASED DIPLAY OF TABS BASED ON UEG SENTENCE RULES[BASE_SET_HIDDEN]
USELESS	ADJECTTIVE_TAB, #-> CONTEXT BASED DIPLAY OF TABS BASED ON UEG SENTENCE RULES[BASE_SET_HIDDEN]
#MEMORY_TABS
	ACTIVE_MEMORY, #Slots = Constitution + Aptitude + Muscle Memory RUMORS, QUESTS, REQUESTS,
	PASSIVE_MEMORY, #Seen, Heard, Felt (STORES PERCEPTION ACTION EVENTS THAT AREN'T NOISE)	
#PROCESSING_TAB->ACCESSED THROUGH TOOL
	CRAFT, 
#CRAFTING_SELECTION/MENUBAR
	TOOL, #ADDITIONAL
	MATERIALS, #MULTI
	ACTION, #TO BE PERFORMED
	SET, # VECTOR [MUST PLACE ATLEAST 2 FOR CUT, 1 FOR HOLE PUNCH/HAMMER]/SHAPE/DIMENSION((L + W)(IF NO VECTORS/OR SKIP) + H (DEPTH)) -> ALL ARE OPTIONAL EXCEPT DEPTH AND/OR SHAPE, TRAIL_HAND_BLADE_POSITION(FOR CHISELING)
	WORKTIMER, #SAME AS REST TIMER
	SAVE_RECIPE, #WHOLE LOOP SHOULD BE SET FIRST
#CRAFTING_ENUM
	MARK, #VECTOR  POINT FOR CRAFTING
	BATCH_ITEM, Create Multiples of one item
	MULTI_ITEM, Create Multiple item types -> preload [loop menu]
# CUT-> FOLLOW VECTOR LINE (SET DEPTH), PIERCE -> PUNTCURES WITH POINT AS TARGET CENTER (SET DEPTH), HIT -> IF LINE-IMPACTS ALONG LINE (SET DEPTH)

enum PlantSubclass_Type {
    HERB,       // Short plants with soft, green stems
    SHRUB,      // Medium woody plants with multiple branches
    TREE,       // Tall plants with a single woody trunk
    CLIMBER,    // Plants requiring support to grow vertically
    CREEPER,    // Plants with fragile stems that grow along the ground
    GRASS       // Graminoids with hollow or flat stems
};

enum DrugPoisonEffectType {
    CORROSIVE,       # Damages organs on contact (acid burns, necrosis)
    IRRITANT,        # Causes itchiness, swelling, general discomfort
    SYSTEMIC,        # Enters bloodstream, affects multiple organs
    NEUROTOXIC,      # Targets nervous system, paralysis, spasms
    CYANOGENIC,      # Produces cyanide; blocks oxygen, rapid suffocation
    CARDIOTOXIC,     # Affects heart and blood pressure
    HEPATOTOXIC,     # Affects liver/related metabolism
    NEPHROTOXIC,     # Affects kidneys/filtration
    GI_TRACT,        # Targets stomach/intestines, vomiting/diarrhea
    HEMOTOXIC,       # Damages blood, causes hemorrhage
    ENZYME_INHIBITOR,# Inhibits key enzymes, may block digestion/nerves
    HALLUCINOGENIC,  # Induces hallucinations, confusion
    DERMATOLOGIC,    # Skin-specific reactions (burns, blisters, rash)
    RESPIRATORY,     # Targets lungs or airway
    COAGULANT,       # Thickens blood (decreases flow)
    ANTICOAGULANT,   # Prevents blood clotting (increases bleeding)
    IMMUNOTOXIC,     # Weakens immune response
    ALLERGEN,        # Triggers allergic reaction
    METABOLIC,       # Disturbs core metabolism (hypoglycemia/hyperglycemia/shock)
    PSYCHOACTIVE,    # Alters mood/thoughts; similar to "Hallucinogenic" but less severe
    CHOLINERGIC,     # Nervous system overload (sweating, salivation, seizures)
    VASODILATOR,     # Opens blood vessels, causes blood pressure drop
    MUCOSAL,         # Damages mucous membranes (mouth, throat, gut)
    CYTOTOXIC,       # Damages cells directly, causes cell death
    RADIOTOXIC,      # Causes radiation-related harm (for monsters/magical ecology)
},

enum DrugPoisonAccumulationType {
    SLOW_ACTING,     # Delayed onset poison
    ACUTE,           # Immediate rapid poisoning
    CUMULATIVE,      # Builds up with repeated exposure, long-term effect
},

	HIGH, #[5-7][POSITIVE =RICH, FULL, SHARP],[NEGATIVE = NEGATIVE]

enum Poly_Synthesis {#Polymerization-trait ->fix logicAIaaddeed BS
#[Mechanism: Material_component]
  		CONDENSTION, #["Creates Peptide/Glycosidic bonds; releases H2O. (Collagen, Cellulose, Silk)]
      		ADDITION, #[Chain growth via radical/enzymatic activation; no byproduct. (Certain Resins/Lipids)]
#[Termination_n]
      FIXED, #[n is a constant blueprint (e.g., Collagen n≈1050). Result: Uniformity.]
      ENVIRONMENTAL, #[n stops based on resource/climate availability. Result: Divergent Growth.",REGIONAL- avg Caloric Value of vegetation - avg CALORIC Need of Species- [Avg Need of Competitors], Competitors = Same diet + Predators
      LINKS, #[Chains bond laterally (e.g., Keratin with Sulfur). Result: High Hardness/Toughness]
#[Genotypes]
    #Fidelity
      FIDELITY_MULIPLIER, #[1.2x Texture_Intensity]
      FIDELITY_EXPRESSION, #[QUALITY:links to adjectives]
    #Velocity
      VELOCITY_MULIPLIER, "0.75x Growth_Time",
      VELOCITY_EXPRESSION, "Rapid assembly of 'n' at the cost of durability; prone to 'Defects' trait."
}

enum Genetic_Formation_Logic {
#[Development: Core_Blueprint]
  INHERITANCE, #["2 sets of chromosomes -1 from each parent" are provided; only one set determines initial trait expression. (Autosomes 1-22, Sex Chromosome 23)]
  EXPRESSION, #["Phenotype = Build, Appearance, Race, Genetic-Conditions, Genetic-Mutations"] are determined by the selected genes and their interactions.
  POLYPLOIDY, #["Number of chromosome sets"] which determines baseline size and fertility characteristics of the species. (e.g., Diploid 2n, Tetraploid 4n).

#[Material_Synthesis: Stages]
  CONDENSATION_SYNTHESIS, #["Creates Peptide/Glycosidic bonds; releases H2O."] Mechanism for creating structural proteins like **Collagen Type I**, **Alpha-Keratin**, and **Cellulose**.
  ADDITION_SYNTHESIS, #["Chain growth via radical/enzymatic activation; no byproduct."] Mechanism for creating lipids, **Squalene**, and many specific alkaloids like **Caffeine** and **Morphine**.
  LINKING_SYNTHESIS, #["Chains bond laterally (e.g., Keratin with Sulfur)."] Mechanism used for strong structural components like **Beta-Keratin**, **Peptidoglycan**, and **Calcium Carbonate** composites.

#[Genetic_Result: Trait_Stability]
  FIXED_TRAIT, #["n is a constant blueprint"] where the material length/expression is a constant genetic property (e.g., Collagen, Chitin). Result: Uniformity.
  ENVIRONMENTAL_TRAIT, #["n stops based on resource/climate availability"] where expression is modulated by external factors (e.g., Lanolin, Hemicellulose, Body Fat). Result: Divergent Growth.

#[Mutation_Logic]
    #Outcomes
      BENEFICIAL, #[25% Base Chance: Expands magnitude range upward, grants increased resistance.]
      NEUTRAL,    #[50% Base Chance: Color variation, no mechanical effect.]
      HARMFUL,    #[25% Base Chance: Reduces magnitude range, grants disease susceptibility, developmental defects.]
    #Triggers
      CHANCE_ROLL, #["If slot filled with 2 'non-can-fill'-> Chance Mutation is rolled".]
      DE_NOVO,     #["Spontaneous (De Novo): (0.6% to 0.7%)" chance for new mutations not inherited from parents.]
}

enum Metabolic_Logic {#Genetic-Homeostasis-trait
#[Pathway: Energy_Transformation]
    ANABOLIC,   #["Construction phase; consumes ATP to synthesize complex biomass (Growth/Repair/Storage)."]
    CATABOLIC,  #["Destruction phase; breaks down substrates (Glucose/Lipids) to yield ATP/Heat."]

#[Regulation: Enzyme_Kinetics]
    CONSTITUTIVE, #["Always ON; Baseline metabolites required for cellular life (e.g., Glycolysis)."]
    FACULTATIVE,  #["Trigger-based; activated by In Utero signals or external stress (e.g., Ketosis)."]

#[Termination_Flux]
    HOMEOSTATIC,  #["Fixed set-point; metabolite levels return to a genetic baseline (n=Normal range)."]
    ALLOSTATIC,   #["Variable set-point; adjusts 'n' based on systemic load/threat (e.g., Adrenaline spikes)."]

#[Genetic_Properties]
    #Efficiency (The "Metabolic Engine" Quality)
    EFFICIENCY_MULTIPLIER, #[1.5x ATP_Yield per unit Substrate. Result: High Endurance.]
    THERMAL_EXPRESSION,    #[HEAT_WASTE:links to adjectives (Endothermic vs Ectothermic)]

    #Specialization (The "Chemical Arsenal")
    XENO_DISSIPATION,      #[VELOCITY: Rate of toxin neutralisation. Result: Poison Resistance.]
    SECONDARY_SYNTHESIS,   #[BIO-UNIQUE: Species-specific compounds (e.g., Venoms, Pheromones, Vitamin-C synthesis).]

#[Environmental_Bias]
    RESOURCE_SCARCITY,    #[THRESHOLD: Reduces Basal Metabolic Rate (BMR) to conserve 'n' units.]
    ABUNDANCE_PLASTICITY, #[THRESHOLD: Increases Lipid_Sequestration (Storage) relative to Caloric_Surplus.]
}

enum Shapes  {#MAGIC specific

	NONE,
	PROJECTILE,
	RAY,
	BEAM,
	PARALLEL_BEAM,
	DIVERGENT_BEAM,
	CONVERGENT_BEAM,
	ORB,
	CUBE,
	LUNE,
	TETRAHEDRON,
	TESSERACT,
	HYPERSPHERE,
};

enum Shapes_Subclass {#CRAFTING AND MAGIC

#PROJECTILE
	ARROWHEAD, #[Arrowhead: Length > Width; Depth < 10% Width (Flattened triangular mass)]
	TEARDROP, #[Teardrop: Base Width = Base Height; Length > Width (Radial base to point taper)]
	BLADE, #[Blade: Length >> Width; height < 5% Width]
	CONE, #[Cone: Height > Width (Tapered 3D volume)]
	SLUG, #[Slug: Height = Width (Balanced mass)]		

#CUBE
 	BOX, #[Box: Height = Width = Depth (CORED; Wall < 10% Width)] #If it has volume.
	BLOCK, #[Block: Height = Width = Depth] #If it is solid and heavy.
#SQUARE
	SLAB, #[Slab: Width & Length >> Depth]		
	FRAME, #[Frame: Width = Length; Center Void > 50% Area (CORED; Perimeter only)]			
	PARTITION, #[Screen: Width = Length; Mass/Void = Interdependent (FLUTED; Permeable plane)]
#SPHERE		
	BALL, #[Ball: Radius = 1 ]			
	SHELL, #[Shell: Radius = 1; Wall < 10% Radius (CORED; Enclosure)]			
	LATTICE, #[Lattice: Radius = 1; Mass < 50% Volume (FLUTED; Structural sphere)]
#CIRLCE
	DISK, #[Disk: Diameter = 1]		
	RING, #[Ring: Diameter = 1; Void > 70% Area (CORED; Pure boundary)]			
	WHEEL, #[Wheel: Diameter = 1; Void/Mass = Structural balance (FLUTED; Radial interface)]
#CYLINDER	
	FILAMENT, #[Filament: Length > 3x Radius (SOLID; Longitudinal mass)]
	TUBE, #[Tube: Length > 3x Radius; Wall < 20% Radius (CORED; Longitudinal passage)]	
#LUNE
 	CRESCENT, #[Half_Moon: Arc Thickness < 10% Radius (CORED; Thin arc-skin)] #Frequently used because the moon's phases are the most recognizable examples of this geometry.
	SICKLE, #[Sickle: Arc Thickness > 20% Radius (SOLID; Weighted curve)] #Used if the curve is sharp or suggests a hook-like quality.

#TETRAHEDRON
	TIP, #[Tip: Vertex = x (The point of convergence)]			
	MOLD, #[Mold: Length > Height (CORED; Negative triangular volume)]# to split or hold something.]			
	TRUSS, #[Truss: Length > Height (FLUTED; Triangular skeleton)]
#TRIANGLE/TIP
	WEDGE, #[Wedge: Length > Height (SOLID; The inclined plane)]
	POINT, #[Point: Length >> Width (The potential for penetration)]# used to Pierce
},

enum Shapes_Status {
	MOLDED, #added for casted shapes,#SHAPED
	CORED, #HOLLOW/Remove inner-mass/center-out
	FLUTED, #MASS-MISSING/remove outer-mass/outer-inner
	FLUTED_CORE #inner threaad logic
	BOUND, # TAG FOR ANYTHING FASTENED INCLUDING ENTITIES
);

var BLADE_EDGE = #OF EDGES -TOTAL# VertexA + VertexB = x (Length)
var TIP = DamageType.EDGE_PIERCE   # Vertex = x (Convergence)
var BLADE = DamageType.EDGE_SLASH  # Edge Radius

	"SMALL": {
		"min": "0.1m",
		"max": "0.4m"
	},
	"REGULAR": {
		"min": "0.4m",
		"max": "0.9m"
	},
	"GREAT": {
		"min": "0.9m",
		"max": "3.0m" # Logic usually treats 2.0+ as anything higher
	}
};

		"max": "4m"
	},
	"BROAD": {
		"min": "5m",
		"max": "6m" # Logic usually treats 2.0+ as anything higher
	}
}

Vertex 0 = (0,0 point of origin)
Vertex x = (convergence/termination points)
Vertex y = (convergence/termination points)

# PROJECTILE
Slug: Height = Width (Balanced mass)
Cone: Height > Width (Tapered 3D volume)
Arrowhead: Length > Width; Depth < 10% Width (Flattened triangular mass)
Blade: Length >> Width; Depth < 5% Width (Extreme longitudinal extension)
Teardrop: Base Width = Base Height; Length > Width (Radial base to point taper)

# CUBE / SQUARE
Block: Height = Width = Depth (Uniform 3D mass)
Box: Height = Width = Depth (CORED; Wall < 10% Width)
Slab: Width & Length >> Depth (Flat independent mass)
Frame: Width = Length; Center Void > 50% Area (CORED; Perimeter only)
Partition: Width = Length; Mass/Void = Interdependent (FLUTED; Permeable plane)

# SPHERE
Ball: Radius = 1 (SOLID; 100% Fill)
Shell: Radius = 1; Wall < 10% Radius (CORED; Enclosure)
Lattice: Radius = 1; Mass < 50% Volume (FLUTED; Structural sphere)

# CIRCLE
Disk: Diameter = 1 (SOLID; 100% Fill)
Ring: Diameter = 1; Void > 70% Area (CORED; Pure boundary)
Wheel: Diameter = 1; Void/Mass = Structural balance (FLUTED; Radial interface)

# CYLINDER
Rod: Length > 3x Radius (SOLID; Longitudinal mass)
Tube: Length > 3x Radius; Wall < 20% Radius (CORED; Longitudinal passage)

# LUNE
Sickle: Arc Thickness > 20% Radius (SOLID; Weighted curve)
Half_Moon: Arc Thickness < 10% Radius (CORED; Thin arc-skin)

# TETRAHEDRON / TRIANGLE
Tip: Vertex = x (The point of convergence)
Wedge: Length > Height (SOLID; The inclined plane)
Mold: Length > Height (CORED; Negative triangular volume)
Truss: Length > Height (FLUTED; Triangular skeleton)
Point: Length >> Width (The potential for penetration)



Typical Fiber/Yarn Thickness: FILAMENT TEXTILE CLASSIFICATION = 
Sewing: Fine thread, <0.5mm (often as fine as 0.1–0.3mm) = FINE_FIBER
Stitching: Slightly thicker, but still fine, 0.5mm to 1mm = SMALL_FIBER
Braiding: 1mm+ (cords/ropes commonly 2–8mm)		= FIBER
Knitting: 1.5mm (fine)–5mm (bulky); most usage 2–4mm = THICK_FIBER


Fastener Shear & Stability (L/W/H Logic)
The stability of a Composite is determined by the Fastener Grade relative to the Part Dimensions.
Fastener	Physics Role	Strength Formula (Sim Logic)
Rivet	Shear Specialist	Strength = (Material_Hardness * Rivet_Area) * Vibration_Modifier(1.0)
Screw	Tension/Torque	Strength = (Thread_Depth * Clamp_Force) * Vibration_Modifier(0.8)
Rope/String	Tensile Binding	Strength = (Tensile_Limit * Knot_Efficiency) * Elasticity_Modifier(< 1.0) [Base_Knot_Efficiency = SURVIVAL SKILL x .5]
Nail Strength Formula: Strength = (Material_Hardness * Surface_Area) * Friction_Coefficient
Stability Logic: Joint_Stability = (Sum_Fastener_Strength) / (Part_Mass * Distance_from_Center).

The Decision-Weight BreakdownBased on your logic, the AI’s decision to build an "Abstract" (like your ladder or cannon) would look something like this:WeightFactorLogic / Game Rule50%Resource CostDoes the Material exist nearby? + How much Stamina/Time does the Refinement_Type (e.g., Knapping/Binding) cost?20%Goal DeadlineHow many turns until the target moves or the "World Event" (from your Hard Difficulty) triggers?20%Handling SkillDoes the character's Aptitude or Muscle Memory allow them to hit the required Joint_Stability on the first try?10%ComplexityHow many "Logical Steps" (from your Intelligence stat) are required to turn the raw material into the functional shape?

AI LOGIC
Problem solving Steps in a chain-> Max 3 ->number of links = infinite (in theory)-> 1.Identify [Problem& solution], 2. Verify/Confirm[Problem is cause not symptom, Solution - Best vs Most efficent/quick], 3. Plan -> Create 3 steps to solve problem ->CHAIN 2 (Same Rules) ->SOULUTION CHAIN-> Repeat CHAIN 1. or  Problem solving Steps in a chain-> Max 3 ->number of links = infinite (in theory)-> 1.Identify [Problem& solution], 2. Verify/Confirm[Problem is cause not symptom, Solution - Best vs Most efficent/quick], 3. Plan -> Create 3 steps to solve problem->Nest Chains into Smaller Steps ->CHAIN 2 (Same Rules) ->SOULUTION CHAIN-> Repeat CHAIN 1. Both Rationales would be valid. Aptitude would determine which one you get, above or below avg. Rationale would determine how many Link of the 3 Link chain you can reason for a LOGOS, PATTHOS, and ETHOS oriented problem. Logos only determines links for logical decision making, meaning technical. social decision chains are governed by Pathos, and expertise/job decision chain is driven by Ethos meaning Aptitude is only for logos chains where charisma would govern pathos and the individual skill would govern ethos for any situation performance/knowledge related


CONVERSIONTABLE global
extends Node

# Your constant table of scales
const UNIT_TABLE = {
	# Measure
	"mm": 0.001,
	"cm": 0.01,
	"m":  1.0,
	"km": 1000.0

	# Weights (Base: 1 kg = 1.0)
	"kg":   1.0,        # Base weight
	"g":    0.001,      # 1,000g in a kg
	"mg":   0.000001,   # 1,000,000mg in a kg
	
	# Liquid (Base: 1L = 1kg of water)
	"l":    1.0,        # 1 Liter of water = 1 kg
	"ml":   0.001,      # 1 mL = 1 g = 0.001 kg
	"dram": 0.003697    # 1 Dram = 3.697 mL = 0.003697 kg

	# Currency (Base: 1 Sila / 1 Liter = 1.0)
	# All weight is calculated relative to the Sila/Grain baseline
	"sila":   1.0,            # Base unit of the economy
	"ban":    10.0,           # 10 Sila
	"gur":    300.0,          # 300 Sila
	"mina":   0.504,          # Weight base from chart
	"shekel": 0.504 / 60.0,   # 1/60th of a Mina
	"talent": 0.504 * 60.0,   # 60 Minas

	# Metal Ratios (1g = Sila grain)
	"gold_val":   0.79,       # 1g Gold ≈ 0.79 kg grain
	"silver_val": 0.066,      # 1g Silver ≈ 0.066 kg grain
	"copper_val": 0.0016      # 1g Copper ≈ 0.0016 kg grain
},

# Your universal math operators
const MATH_OPS = {
	"+float%": func(f: float): return f * 0.1,
	"-float%": func(f: float): return -1.0 * f * 0.1,
	# You can add others here, e.g., "half": func(f): return f * 0.5
};

# Universal Range Checker
func is_in_range(current_val: float, descriptor: int, mod_str: String, data_map: Dictionary) -> bool:
	# 1. Get base float from the specific dictionary passed in (Moods, Dispo, etc)
	var base_f = data_map.get(descriptor, 0.0)
	
	# 2. Resolve the threshold using the global math operator
	var threshold = 0.0
	if MATH_OPS.has(mod_str):
		threshold = MATH_OPS[mod_str].call(base_f)
	else:
		threshold = base_f # Fallback to raw value if no modifier
	
	# 3. Universal Comparison (Logic from your design)
	if threshold >= 0:
		return current_val >= threshold
	return current_val <= threshold


# The "Parser" function that makes the number
func n(input: String) -> float:
	var value = input.to_float() # Grabs the "2" from "2cm"
	
	# Logic to find the unit string (the "cm")
	for unit in UNIT_TABLE.keys():
		if input.ends_with(unit):
			return value * UNIT_TABLE[unit] # Does the math for you
			
	return value # Fallback if no unit found

"-float%": -1 * float * .1
"+float%": 1 * float * .1
};

# Attributes
enum Attribute {
	STRENGTH, #[Torso = 50% of strength stat, Arms = 10% of strength stat each, Legs = 15% of strength stat, = Power 40%,  Stamina 40%, Toughness 20%]
	INTELLIGENCE, #[Tied to Head[50%] and Internal [stomach[25%] & brain[25%]] = Charisma 10%, Muscle Memory 20%, Aptitude 70%]
	ENDURANCE, #[Tied to Internal [lungs[33%], muscle[33%], and fat[33%]] = Stamina 50%, Quickness 15%, Muscle Memory 15%, Constution 20%]
	DEXTERITY, #[Tied to Hands[50%] and Internal [eyes[50%]] = Accuracy 50%, Quickness 25%, Muscle Memory 25%]
	WILLPOWER, #[Tied to Internal [brain] = Toughness 25%, Resilience 25%, Aptitude 20%, Constitution 30%]
	PERCEPTION, #[Tied to Internal [Eyes[25%], Ears[25%], Nose[25%], Skin[25%]] = Accuracy 50%, Charisma 20%, Resilience 15%,  Aptitude 15%]
	HEIGHT, #(in cm) = used for metabolism and body comp calculations]
	WINGSPAN, # Wingspan (avg) = Height [arm length]
}

enum JudgementType {
	TRIAL,
EVIDENTIAL,
	DE_FACTO, #A JUDGE ALONE ACTS AS THE "FINDER OF FACT," MAKING THE FINAL DECISION WITHOUT A JURY.
	JURY, #GROUP OF PEERS (USUALLY 6–12 CITIZENS) EVIDENCE AND RENDERS A VERDICT.
	WITNESS, #(Testimony type 1) A GROUP OF 1ST HAND ACCOUNTS (USUALLY >OR=2 CITIZENS) LISTENS TO EVIDENCE AND RENDERS A VERDICT. IN SYSTEMS LIKE ANCIENT ROME OR ISLAMIC SHARIA, THE VERDICT RELIED ON THE DIRECT OBSERVATION OF A REQUIRED NUMBER OF HONORABLE WITNESSES (OFTEN TWO) WHO PROVIDED "FIRST-HAND ACCOUNTS".
	COMPURGATION, #(TRIAL BY OATH)(Testimony type 2, friends) THE ACCUSED ESTABLISHED INNOCENCE BY GATHERING A SET NUMBER OF "OATH-HELPERS" (COMPURGATORS) WHO SWORE TO THEIR CHARACTER AND THE TRUTH OF THEIR DENIAL. IT WAS A TEST OF SOCIAL CREDIT AND SPIRITUAL FEAR OF PERJURY.
	INQUEST, #(Testimony type 3- Nonassociates)EARLY MEDIEVAL PRECURSORS TO JURIES WHERE A GROUP OF LOCAL MEN WAS SUMMONED TO SPEAK "THE TRUTH" (VEREDICTUM) BASED ON THEIR PERSONAL KNOWLEDGE OF THE FACTS OR THE NEIGHBORHOOD'S REPUTATION
ACTIONABLE,
	COMBAT, #(WAGER OF BATTLE)A JUDICIAL DUEL BETWEEN THE ACCUSER AND THE ACCUSED (OR THEIR CHAMPIONS). IT WAS BASED ON THE PREMISE THAT GOD WOULD GRANT VICTORY TO THE RIGHTEOUS PARTY, REGARDLESS OF PHYSICAL STRENGTH.
	ORDEAL, #(JUDICIUM DEI)AN APPEAL TO DIVINE INTERVENTION WHERE THE ACCUSED UNDERWENT A PHYSICAL TEST (FIRE, WATER, INGESTION). SURVIVAL OR HEALING WAS VIEWED AS A MIRACULOUS "VERDICT" FROM GOD.
},

Formulas- 


*[note-to-self][Formulas 1. need to be organized, 2. need to be paired with heat-transfer formula, and all should be coded into a state machine.(instead of running for minor changes, its main use will be for fire and magic simulation so only intentional state changes are calculated, -ps- Consider adding a buffer script for weather-mechanic (other optionis static range rolls based on season, but math is done for simulation below.
